Comments From wernerlau.com: This is one of our top dive sites, located to the east of Mulee Island. During the season from May to December mantas can almost always be seen with their offspring, busying themselves around the numerous cleaning stations at 10 - 15 metres. The gentle slope, from 15 - 30 metres, is adorned with coral formations and is the home of barracuda, napoleons, sharks and tuna. This spot is a natural meeting ground for numerous other big fish. In ideal currents it is a dream to dive here.
